  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_a946eab5-5aba-4c43-98ac-dd442df9e356'
      });
    }

  <span id="freeText759945728105571892" style="display:none">A brilliant, hilarious one-off novella in the Skulduggery Pleasant universe, from number-one-bestselling author Derek Landy<br /><br />This time, the bad guys take the stage.<br /><br />Tanith Low, now possessed by a remnant, recruits a gang of villains – many of whom will be familiar from previous Skulduggery adventures – in order to track down and steal the four God-Killer level weapons that could hurt Darquesse when she eventually emerges. Also on the trail of the weapons is a secret group of Sanctuary sorcerers, and doing his best to keep up and keep Tanith alive is one Mister Ghastly Bespoke.<br /><br />When the villains around her are lying and scheming and plotting, Tanith needs to stay two steps ahead of her teammates and her enemies. After all, she's got her own double-crosses to plan – and she’s a villain herself…</span>

<div class='questionText'>
<a href="/questions/903206-can-this-be-read-as-a-standalone-novel">Can this be read as a standalone novel?</a>
</div>
<div class='communityQAFooter questionFooter'>
<ul class='questionFooterActions'>
<li class='footerItem like'>
<span class='likeItContainer' id='like_container_community_question_903206'><a rel="nofollow" class="jsLike like_it" href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/new?remember=true&amp;return_url=%2Fbook%2Fshow%2F16119044-the-maleficent-seven">like</a></span>

</li>
<li class='footerItem communityQuestionTimestamp'>
<a href="/questions/903206-can-this-be-read-as-a-standalone-novel">4 years ago</a>

<div class='allCommunityAnswers'>
<div class='communityAnswer'>
<div class='communityAnswerBody'>
<div class='answererUserIcon'>
<a class="leftAlignedImage userPhoto" href="/user/show/32665633-cordelia-shirley"><img alt="" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/users/1480544189i/32665633._UY100_CR25,0,100,100_.jpg" /></a>
</div>
<div class='communityAnswerTextContainer'>
<span class='communityAnswererName'>
<a href="/user/show/32665633-cordelia-shirley">Cordelia Shirley</a>
</span>
<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">Probably. There are references to other things that have happened in the novels, but they're pretty clearly explained, so it wouldn't interfere with y<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">Probably. There are references to other things that have happened in the novels, but they're pretty clearly explained, so it wouldn't interfere with your understanding of the plot. However, you might be missing out on a few inside jokes that have been thrown in. I'd recommend reading the rest of the series so you can get to know the characters better (and because it's just an awesome series!), but I don't think it's ENTIRELY necessary!<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>
</div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer473934608" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17776771096532808225">Oh, Tanith!! All I wanted to whilst reading this book was reach through the pages and wrap her in a big, big hug. But the only person that got to do that was Sanguine...and that just depressed me. The sooner they find a way to rid Tanith of the Remnant, the better!   <span id="freeText4897931221123477789" style="display:none"><b>While my insides may be rotten, I still like a good reason to kill someone. It has to be either business, personal, or out of sheer boredom. </b><br /><br />I'm usually not one for novella's usually as they don't really add much to the plot of the main story however this one provided some context of one of the series main characters Tanith Low who has a remnant inside of her. <br /><br />Seeing many of the underrated and missed villains finally getting to shine throughout this novella and see them do what villains do best and is cause mayhem. But i love how plotting and scheming she is in this book and it's so out of character due to the remnant in her but man it was so fun to read at times. <br /><br />I did really enjoy getting to see Tanith adventures in this little novella away from the main series as she wasn't really scene much in book seven. </span>

<div id="review_576911824" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/576911824" />
    <a title="Becky" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1978609-becky"><img alt="Becky" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1233429155p2/1978609.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/576911824?book_show_action=true">Mar 31, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Becky" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Becky" href="/user/show/1978609-becky">Becky</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer576911824" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13307931777199517390">It's here!!! It's finally here, another book from the masterful Derek Landy. I got this as an Easter present today and got stuck right in. Of course I finished it in a mere few hours. Derek Landy is one of those authors who I will drop EVERYTHING for! My reading pile may be 200 or so books long, but his books will jump to the top everytime. They are just kick butt awesome.<br/>This book is a spin off novella, told a couple of months after the events in Kingdom of the Wicked, but this time the story i</span>
  <span id="freeText13307931777199517390" style="display:none">It's here!!! It's finally here, another book from the masterful Derek Landy. I got this as an Easter present today and got stuck right in. Of course I finished it in a mere few hours. Derek Landy is one of those authors who I will drop EVERYTHING for! My reading pile may be 200 or so books long, but his books will jump to the top everytime. They are just kick butt awesome.<br />This book is a spin off novella, told a couple of months after the events in Kingdom of the Wicked, but this time the story is told from Tanith's side of things and she's a bad guy now.<br />At 280 pages this is quite short but still packed with so much awesomeness. I always loved Tanith - she's one of my favourite characters, I still wish she would come back to the good side, but I will admit she makes quite a cool villain. This book also reveals some of her past which I found fascinating and it was good to see that history.<br />Tanith is trying to track down, steal and destroy four weapons that can kill with a single nick, they are called 'God Killer's' as nothing can stop them, she recruits a band of villains to help her, some are known favourites from earlier books such as Billy-Ray, Springheeled Jack and Dusk, whilst others are new additions. all with very different talents, and some more disgusting than others.<br />I got so excited whist reading this as one of the new characters has the same surname as me, I am being delusional and telling myself that Derek Landy did that deliberately, just for me. The character is male and I am of course female, but Derek can't be too obvious can he? :P I know it's a tribute to one of his most dedicated fans!!! :D<br />There is a distinct lack of Skulduggery and Valkyrie in this book, but in a strange way it works, Tanith is such a strong character that she commands the page and captures the story.<br />I don't want to write too much about it as I don't want to give away any spoilers, just know that this book is just as incredible as all the others and yes I did laugh out loud in many places.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13307931777199517390" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_444825279" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5117138-kribu?shelf=action">action</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5117138-kribu?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5117138-kribu?shelf=skeleton">skeleton</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5117138-kribu?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5117138-kribu?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer444825279" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8794153320093312549">ETA: Re-read; review below unchanged.<br/><br/>I admit: I expected this book to be fluffy fun, but considering that it's essentially a side story in the <i>Skulduggery Pleasant</i> universe, focusing entirely on secondary characters and not even featuring either Skulduggery or Valkyrie, my expectations were, well, somewhat limited.<br/><br/>Oh boy. Was I wrong.<br/><br/>Right now - admittedly, I'm still on that high from finishing it - I'd rank it as one of the very best of the entire SP series. It's shorter than the main series no</span>
  <span id="freeText8794153320093312549" style="display:none">ETA: Re-read; review below unchanged.<br /><br />I admit: I expected this book to be fluffy fun, but considering that it's essentially a side story in the <i>Skulduggery Pleasant</i> universe, focusing entirely on secondary characters and not even featuring either Skulduggery or Valkyrie, my expectations were, well, somewhat limited.<br /><br />Oh boy. Was I wrong.<br /><br />Right now - admittedly, I'm still on that high from finishing it - I'd rank it as one of the very best of the entire SP series. It's shorter than the main series novels, yes, but being still novel-length, it fit in more than enough - plot, some <i>excellent</i> character stuff, back stories for several characters, lots of action and even a fair bit of romance (hey, it even has a love triangle of sorts - and anyone who knows me even a bit knows what I think about love triangles in general, but this being Derek, it was awesome, as usual).<br /><br />The feels. Ye gads, the feels this book gave me. I officially managed to fall in love with Springheeled Jack. I loved the banter, both among the good guys and the bad guys. I enjoyed the action. I ... there are twists, towards the end, that I did not see coming. I came pretty damn close to tears at one of them. <br /><br />I think this is as close as I can get to a "review" without getting into spoiler territory, and I just don't want to do that right now. But... yeah. Awesome. <br /><br />I'm terrified of Last Stand of Dead Men, now. Not that I wasn't before, but... yeah.</span>
  <a data-text-id="8794153320093312549" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_648433482" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/648433482" />
    <a title="colleen the convivial curmudgeon" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1209800-colleen-the-convivial-curmudgeon"><img alt="colleen the convivial curmudgeon" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1572581488p2/1209800.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/648433482?book_show_action=true">Jun 22, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="colleen the convivial curmudgeon" class="user" itemprop="url" name="colleen the convivial curmudgeon" href="/user/show/1209800-colleen-the-convivial-curmudgeon">colleen the convivial curmudgeon</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780007512379" href="/book/show/17470683-the-maleficent-seven">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1209800-colleen-the-convivial-curmudgeon?shelf=dark-fantasy">dark-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1209800-colleen-the-convivial-curmudgeon?shelf=action-adventure">action-adventure</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1209800-colleen-the-convivial-curmudgeon?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer648433482" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11578937127485399736">2.5<br/><br/>Based on the mostly 4 & 5 star ratings and gushing reviews, I'm definitely in the minority on this one, but I just had a hard time getting into it.<br/><br/>Maybe part of it was disappointed expectations. When I first heard about this book I was all geared up to love it. I mean, I like Tanith and I always like when the villains - even villains you're hoping will end back up on the good side - get a bit more depth to their characters.<br/><br/>And we did learn more about Tanith, specifically her upbringing and be</span>
  <span id="freeText11578937127485399736" style="display:none">2.5<br /><br />Based on the mostly 4 &amp; 5 star ratings and gushing reviews, I'm definitely in the minority on this one, but I just had a hard time getting into it.<br /><br />Maybe part of it was disappointed expectations. When I first heard about this book I was all geared up to love it. I mean, I like Tanith and I always like when the villains - even villains you're hoping will end back up on the good side - get a bit more depth to their characters.<br /><br />And we did learn more about Tanith, specifically her upbringing and being trained as an assassin and then giving that up to become a mercenary, of sorts, and then a bounty hunter. Basically, Tanith before we ever meet her in Skulduggery.<br /><br />And those bits were interesting and, honestly, if that was the whole of the story I probably would've rated this higher.<br /><br />But those bits were just interludes in the story of the Maleficent Seven - a group that Tanith puts together in order to track down 4 weapons - God-killers - because she's seen a vision of Darquesse and she, or the Remnant within her, wants to help bring about that destruction.<br /><br />Against them is a team of seven of the good guys, lead by Dexter Vex, who are also after the weapons, but to secure their use against Darquesse.<br /><br />And so, basically, we get a lot of scheming, fighting, chasing from both sides - rinse, wash, repeat.<br /><br />The good guys were hard to root for because they basically seemed kind of inept. Valkyrie and Skulduggery aren't in the book at all, mentioned only in passing, and I almost feel like they couldn't be in the book because we couldn't have a story in which our two main heros would be quite as blundering as our good guys were.<br /><br />In some ways, it was like a typical story of this kind where the bad guys are pretty inept, but at least you want them to sort of be inept because you want the good guys to win. But, in this story, you'd almost have to root for Tanith and Co. because, well, they are the protagonists, in a way... but I kept wanting them to fail.<br /><br />There are some stories written from the villains perspective that makes them more sympathetic, or likable, or where you get into their heads and at least sort of understand where they're coming from. But Remnant Tanith is just a psychopath and so is Billy-Ray. I kinda liked some of the rest of the villain group - it was cool to see Spring-Heeled Jack and Black Annis again, for instance, but they never seemed to be used to their full capacity and then, well... <br /><br />That was one thing. On at least two occassions Tanith went into retrieve the weapon herself and I kept thinking - why did we even both putting together a team? They were all involved in the last encounter, for the most part, so there is that. <br /><br />But, anyway... kind of a lackluster story in which I kept hoping the main characters would fail and/or that the 'good guys' would be more competent and at least put up a bit of a fight.<br /><br />I did like the background on Tanith, and I liked the ending, and the rest was "ok". </span>
  <a data-text-id="11578937127485399736" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Kristy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13971560-kristy"><img alt="Kristy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1596232903p2/13971560.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/547140325?book_show_action=true">Feb 26, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristy" href="/user/show/13971560-kristy">Kristy</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780007512379" href="/book/show/17470683-the-maleficent-seven">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13971560-kristy?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13971560-kristy?shelf=the-hoard">the-hoard</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13971560-kristy?shelf=middle-grade">middle-grade</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer547140325" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6826708660600976485"><b>Holy shitballs, was that a 3-star rating I just gave to a <i>Skulduggery</i> book? YOU BET YOUR SWEET ASS IT WAS!</b><br/><br/>Settle down and let me explain. I love this series. I <i>adore</i> it. I've had so much fun re-reading it, but honestly I think I burnt myself out a bit from reading through the series back-to-back.<br/><br/>I started my re-read of <i>The Maleficent Seven</i> a month ago. A WHOLE MONTH! This book is by no means a long book. In fact, it's the smallest in the series (if you don't include <i>The End of the World</i>, that is</span>
  <span id="freeText6826708660600976485" style="display:none"><b>Holy shitballs, was that a 3-star rating I just gave to a <i>Skulduggery</i> book? YOU BET YOUR SWEET ASS IT WAS!</b><br /><br />Settle down and let me explain. I love this series. I <i>adore</i> it. I've had so much fun re-reading it, but honestly I think I burnt myself out a bit from reading through the series back-to-back.<br /><br />I started my re-read of <i>The Maleficent Seven</i> a month ago. A WHOLE MONTH! This book is by no means a long book. In fact, it's the smallest in the series (if you don't include <i>The End of the World</i>, that is). And only partway through, I fell into a massive slump. Yep. I'm pretty sure this is the first book I've finished in over a month. I'm sure you all know what happens when you fall into a slump partway through a book, right? <i>You lose interest.</i><br /><br />I guess it didn't help that whilst this is set in the world of <i>Skulduggery Pleasant</i>, this by no means a tale involving the skeleton detective. I love Tanith, but I just can't connect to this story like I do with all of the other books.<br /><br />Throughout my re-reading, I've been enjoying getting to parts and being all like, "omg yessssss I remember this!!!" and looking forward to other bits and pieces I remember happening. Tbh, I didn't remember anything about this book at all. It almost felt like reading it for the first time, but not necessarily in a good way.<br /><br />I think if I hadn't fallen into a slump whilst reading this, I would've given it a solid 4 or maybe even 4.5 rating, but instead it's just gonna sit at a 3.5.</span>
  <a data-text-id="6826708660600976485" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 000753194X" href="/book/show/25089472-the-maleficent-seven">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21514123-natalie?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21514123-natalie?shelf=action">action</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3240840224" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6650763902106125549">4.5 / 5<br/><br/><i>"Two monsters, a vampire, a hitman and a ninja, plus whatever this mystery woman is. You know what this means? We're going to die. We are going. To die."<br/>"Don't be so dramatic."</i><br/><br/>Oh boy, this book is not at <i>all</i> what I thought it was, and was certainly a bit more violent and "backstabby" than I thought it was going to be. Wow O.O<br/><br/>In this, we have two groups of seven facing off against one another in a plot to steal four "God Killer" weapons from various people (and groups) around the world, fi</span>
  <span id="freeText6650763902106125549" style="display:none">4.5 / 5<br /><br /><i>"Two monsters, a vampire, a hitman and a ninja, plus whatever this mystery woman is. You know what this means? We're going to die. We are going. To die."<br />"Don't be so dramatic."</i><br /><br />Oh boy, this book is not at <i>all</i> what I thought it was, and was certainly a bit more violent and "backstabby" than I thought it was going to be. Wow O.O<br /><br />In this, we have two groups of seven facing off against one another in a plot to steal four "God Killer" weapons from various people (and groups) around the world, fighting against both time and each other in a bid to retrieve the only weapons <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[...aside from a certain sceptre that a certain reflection has... <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> that could kill <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Darquesse <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. One group to <i>save</i> said person, and one group to <i>kill</i> said person. <br /><br /><i>"We could wear disguises."<br />"Like a false beard. I've always wanted to wear a false beard."<br />"But you're a woman."<br />"Exactly. They'd never suspect it was me."</i><br /><br />I also really loved the flashbacks to a younger Tanith - when she was learning to be a "hidden blade" in some sort of underground assassin-training school that reminds me a bit of the Faceless Men (from Game of Thrones, not to be confused with the <i>Faceless Ones</i> from Skulduggery Pleasant ;D). Getting to learn about how she became the badass she's been since the beginning of the Skulduggery Pleasant was a real treat, and I would love to learn even more about her background. <br /><br /><i>"...I didn't kill him. Besides, I have an alibi. Probably. When did he die?"<br />"Halloween."<br />"I have no alibi."</i><br /><br />There's definitely some set-up here for the future books; definitely not just a side story <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[especially with what Billy-Ray now has... <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I'm hoping that the plot twist at the end of this is going to come into play in one of the later books, rather than staying solely as a side-story. It'll be interesting to find out how things go down later... <br /><br />As per usual [for Derek Landy] the book was incredible (even with it being so short in comparison to others in the world of Skulduggery Pleasant), full of action and plot twists and the ever present (and wonderful) comedy and sarcasm that these characters [and the author] are known for. The whole thing was just incredibly well done - and incredibly vicious - especially with some of those final twists... Wow o.o<br /><br /><i>"...I don't limit myself because of what I am," he said as he walked away. "Do you?"</i></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9780007500925" href="/book/show/16119043-tanith-low-in-the-maleficent-seven">review of another edition</a>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer2137358490" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer2018047309893296531">1. Why did I decide to read this book?<br/><br/>I heard about the skulduggery series but I never really paid much attention to it until I stumbled upon it in the library. The cover seemed so fascinating and the summary at the back was so interesting especially how it said, "it's a good day to be a bad guy." <br/><br/>2. Why I didn't like it:<br/><br/>I wouldn't say that I didn't like it, but I also feel like there were some things that tipped me off this book than things that were good about it. I couldn't keep up with all t</span>
  <span id="freeText2018047309893296531" style="display:none">1. Why did I decide to read this book?<br /><br />I heard about the skulduggery series but I never really paid much attention to it until I stumbled upon it in the library. The cover seemed so fascinating and the summary at the back was so interesting especially how it said, "it's a good day to be a bad guy." <br /><br />2. Why I didn't like it:<br /><br />I wouldn't say that I didn't like it, but I also feel like there were some things that tipped me off this book than things that were good about it. I couldn't keep up with all the characters and the plot only got interesting in the middle of the book when real action started happening. (My opinion) Also, there was a lot more blood and gore than I expected. I'm not the biggest fan when it comes to these kinds of scenes in books. And, the author described it TOO well. OK, maybe that was a good thing. Other than that it was a decent book to read.<br /><br />3. Something new I learned from this book:<br /><br />Although this was a fiction book, I learnt that parents in their society leave their children behind so that they can be trained. But only if the child/children have powers. <br /><br />4. A character that was interesting to me in this book and why:<br /><br />I liked the main character Tanith Low because although an evil entity has grown in her, the author portrays her as a good character. It's like a bipolar, evil superhero. She leads the team and is very wise when making decisions. She's a character I can look up to. In the book, there would be chapters where it's just a childhood memory of her in training. You can see how it connects back to her in the present because her personality traits now are the effects of those events back then. She's strong, charming and can talk her way out of things. She represents girl power and is not afraid to man up to a challenge. </span>
  <a data-text-id="2018047309893296531" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_498700570" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/498700570" />
    <a title="Ela" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7930364-ela"><img alt="Ela" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1517604999p2/7930364.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/498700570?book_show_action=true">Jan 07, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ela" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ela" href="/user/show/7930364-ela">Ela</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Ela by: </span>
      Nick
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7930364-ela?shelf=ya-paranormal-fiction">ya-paranormal-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7930364-ela?shelf=spin-offs">spin-offs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7930364-ela?shelf=action">action</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7930364-ela?shelf=ya">ya</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer498700570" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4850503552682528254">Me when I started this: <i>*sigh* Not really in the mood for Derek Landy right now, but since it's here...</i><br/><br/>Me about half an hour later: <i>DAMN! I remember why I love you now Derek!</i><br/><br/>It's been about a year since I've read a book by Landy and I'd slightly forgotten just how funny and outrageous his stories are. This is one of the best spin offs I've read, Landy's minor characters are interesting enough to easily run their own show with no help from the protagonists (Skuduggery and Valkryie) and have enoug</span>
  <span id="freeText4850503552682528254" style="display:none">Me when I started this: <i>*sigh* Not really in the mood for Derek Landy right now, but since it's here...</i><br /><br />Me about half an hour later: <i>DAMN! I remember why I love you now Derek!</i><br /><br />It's been about a year since I've read a book by Landy and I'd slightly forgotten just how funny and outrageous his stories are. This is one of the best spin offs I've read, Landy's minor characters are interesting enough to easily run their own show with no help from the protagonists (Skuduggery and Valkryie) and have enough depth to provide an engaging storyline. <br /><br />Do I have any criticisms... The only thing I would say is that the Skulduggery series possibly does work better with Valkyrie as the main character; simply because she's a teenager. Given that this is a kids book and the main character is a sociopath who's dating a psychopath, I did feel there were a couple of moments which felt a little...forced, as Landy struggled to keep everything PG (or 12 maybe)<br /><br />However, to Landy's credit, he did manage to do so. Successfully creating yet another ridiculously fierce, wild, complex female lead in Tanith Low. He has managed to stay very true to Tanith's original character while also taking into account the remnant and making her scarily psychotic. So congratulations Derek Landy, this novel is officially a triumph! (As far as I'm concerned anyway)<br /><br />(Also, this was without a doubt one of my favourite covers, front and back. It you haven't seen the back already, just wait till you do, its awesome.)<br /><br />And now some spoiler comments...<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br /><br />Tanith Low might learn to control her Remnant!<br />Billy-Ray has the God-Killers!<br />TANITH AND BILLY ARE GETTING MARRIED!<br /><br /><br />I also cannot believe the comment about Caelan "The boy was a danger to us all. he stalked and he tortured and he murdered every woman he became enamoured with."<br />I know he was psychotic by the end of his relationship with Valkyrie, but I thought that was individual to her or maybe to do with the fact that he was slightly lacking in experience as far as relationships went. But no, turns out he's a mass murderer.<br />Tut tut Val, should have listened to Skulduggery when he warned you.<br /><br /> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>
  <a data-text-id="4850503552682528254" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer18205414755034624248">Actual rate 3.5 stars<br/> When I first saw in HarperCollins website that there will be a novella all about Miss Tanith Low I got SOO SOO SOO excited!! Like come on!! A whole book about evil bad ass possessed Tanith!!!<br/> After waiting for cover and release and the back cover (I KNOW IT'S AMAZING!!), and the book's arrival, I got it and.......... I just didn't read it. Couple of days later read 30 pages and I could not believe the disappointment I got from this book. Any Skulduggery Pleasant reader know</span>
  <span id="freeText18205414755034624248" style="display:none">Actual rate 3.5 stars<br /> When I first saw in HarperCollins website that there will be a novella all about Miss Tanith Low I got SOO SOO SOO excited!! Like come on!! A whole book about evil bad ass possessed Tanith!!!<br /> After waiting for cover and release and the back cover (I KNOW IT'S AMAZING!!), and the book's arrival, I got it and.......... I just didn't read it. Couple of days later read 30 pages and I could not believe the disappointment I got from this book. Any Skulduggery Pleasant reader knows that there are couple of villain chapters along the book. Yes they can sometimes be interesting, sometimes boring to a bearable level, but after all they are just couple of chapters. But in this novella it was the WHOLE BOOK! So I decided that I'm not ready to start such book.<br /> After I finished my final exams I was about early 100s throughout this book and decided just to get it over with. Page after page you get used to the CONDITION of the book and it took me less than 2 days to finish the other 180 pages. The story got more interesting but there were many characters who just entered the picture to make a plot, and when I say many I mean around 9 or more so that was a bit hard to follow. Anyway the book had plenty of funny stuff. maybe more than any book in the original series (compared to the amount of pages).<br /> The end, got to say that the best thing about this book was its last couple of chapters. Really enjoyed it. <br /> Bottom line. Recommended to any Skulduggery Pleasant fan but you can expect some disappointments while reading this book. After all it's just an additional book to the series. So no need to be mad. </span>

  <span id="freeText9851258054983719031" style="display:none">The Skulduggery pleasant series has been spread way too thin and it hasn't been more evident than in this book. The story itself isn't even than interesting, the best part is the backstory about Tanith Low and, again, it's not even that good. But then come the real flaws:<br />1. It's the same humour.       <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Amanda" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Amanda" href="/user/show/7897151-amanda">Amanda</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7897151-amanda?shelf=children-young-adult">children-young-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer611445625" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18126841712174631541">I rated this 5 stars the first time I read it, but I don't remember having actually loved it. It's true that my love for the Skulduggery Pleasant series makes in indiscriminately rate all the books 5 stars. In this case though, I recognized a 3 star book when I reread it. Skulduggery and Valkyrie don't appear in this short novel, which was one of the main reason why I didn't love this. Additionally, this book is about two factions racing to steal the same objects. The team of baddies was so much</span>
  <span id="freeText18126841712174631541" style="display:none">I rated this 5 stars the first time I read it, but I don't remember having actually loved it. It's true that my love for the Skulduggery Pleasant series makes in indiscriminately rate all the books 5 stars. In this case though, I recognized a 3 star book when I reread it. Skulduggery and Valkyrie don't appear in this short novel, which was one of the main reason why I didn't love this. Additionally, this book is about two factions racing to steal the same objects. The team of baddies was so much more charismatic that the team of good guys. I didn't care about the two Dead Men characters, who are supposed to be epic like Skulduggery, and I grew to actively dislike Aurora. Their parts of the story really dragged for me. In the end, I still did enjoy this, but no where near the level of the main books in this series.</span>
  <a data-text-id="18126841712174631541" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer663705447" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14481859610228436995">There are four god killing weapons hidden around the world and good girl turned evil, Tanith Low is after them. So what do you do when you need to undertake a major operation? You put a team together. Meanwhile a group of the good guys has the same idea, though they don't know they are up against the infamous Tanith Low.<br/><br/>This book was so much fun! I laughed out loud in numerous places and sniggered at all the rest. Action packed, a great cast of characters and dialogue to die for, Derek Landy is </span>
  <span id="freeText14481859610228436995" style="display:none">There are four god killing weapons hidden around the world and good girl turned evil, Tanith Low is after them. So what do you do when you need to undertake a major operation? You put a team together. Meanwhile a group of the good guys has the same idea, though they don't know they are up against the infamous Tanith Low.<br /><br />This book was so much fun! I laughed out loud in numerous places and sniggered at all the rest. Action packed, a great cast of characters and dialogue to die for, Derek Landy is king.</span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer2544866416&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2544866416" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6771004528935496495">I really liked this book! Is is a separate book from the series but is still in the universe of Skullduggery. It includes Tanith Low collecting four God-killer weapons to defend a evil that will arrive soon. The ending was a unexpected twist of Tanith escaping her prison and returning to her home. I recommend this book to any fantasy lovers and everyone really!</span>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('NIYQR9HikUnBu2v+zEv03usbDRBRmo9UJyG4VV1+xtkpod7Y+kc51KyF8Ks5jZ3IJZPjygkGsXEm10ZCRiMCxQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('X8UcsE9Dh16ZQd/IZjUrzac7b3ziYRP4zi37SML+nG9C4tIvZOYvw/R/RJ2T80LbabOBprr9Ld3P2wVf2aNYcw==')})
  }
//]]>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer1997149783815543713">Derek Landy is an Irish writer and screenwriter. In addition to the bestselling children's/YA series of <i>Skulduggery Pleasant</i> books, a supernatural mystery series starring Skulduggery Pleasant, a skeleton detective, and Valkyrie Cain, a young female magician, he has written two screenplays that have been made into films: the IFTA award winning "Dead Bodies" and the IFTA nominated "Boy Eats Girl". L</span>
  <span id="freeText1997149783815543713" style="display:none">Derek Landy is an Irish writer and screenwriter. In addition to the bestselling children's/YA series of <i>Skulduggery Pleasant</i> books, a supernatural mystery series starring Skulduggery Pleasant, a skeleton detective, and Valkyrie Cain, a young female magician, he has written two screenplays that have been made into films: the IFTA award winning "Dead Bodies" and the IFTA nominated "Boy Eats Girl". Landy himself was nominated for an IFTA for Best Script. <br /><br />He doesn’t like to brag about all the awards he’s won, such as the Irish Book of the Decade, or the Red House in the UK, or all the other awards that he humbly displays on his mantelpiece. He is also far too modest to mention things like the first book being a Publisher’s Weekly Best Book of the Year, but would like to extend an invitation to Oprah to pop around one day for tea, in thanks for selecting his book for the Oprah’s Book Club Kids Reading List. <br /><br />Derek plays too many video games, reads too many comics, and watches too many movies. He lives in Ireland with too many cats. Occasionally he talks to real people, but only when he absolutely has to.</span>
  <a data-text-id="1997149783815543713" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>
